Let me talk about the facilities in the room:
It is written on Ctrip that it was renovated in 2017, but it should not be all the rooms. The mattress in our room was visibly sunken, and the sleeping comfort was not very high, but the other facilities in the room were well maintained.
Let me talk about the hotel service: (Although the hotel duty manager has given an explanation and apologized by giving breakfast, I still want to say it)
I am a little unhappy. When traveling during the holidays, I just want to sleep until I wake up naturally, whether I stay in a hotel or at home. However, on the morning of the first day of stay, I knocked on the door to wake up the room attendant. Itâ€™s okay to wake up, but the most unacceptable thing for me is that the door was opened directly. Fortunately, the anti-theft chain was hung. This operation made me lose sleep directly and was very uncomfortable.
Otherwise, there is nothing to say. I hope the hotel will not have such service problems again, otherwise the warm and thoughtful service of the young lady the day before yesterday will be completely wiped out because of this.
